### Rules for Conversion of Sentences:

#### 1. If there is a Preposition before an Adjective, then replace it with 'ता' or 'ती'.

Example:
[English]: A good looking man. 
[Hindi]: सुन्नत मान.

#### 2. If there is a Preposition before a Noun, then replace it with 'से' or 'सें'.

Example:
[English]: The man who came yesterday. 
[Hindi]: आज आये का व्यक्ति 

#### 3. If there is a Preposition before a Verb, then replace it with 'के' or 'कें'.

Example:
[English]: The man who came yesterday. 
[Hindi]: आज आये का व्यक्ति 

#### 4. If there is a Preposition before a Pronoun, then replace it with 'के' or 'कें'.

Example:
[English]: He has been arrested by the police. 
[Hindi]: उसने पुलिस के हाथों लगा दिया गया है।

#### 5. If there is a Preposition before a Noun, then replace it with 'के' or 'कें'.

Example:
[English]: I saw him. 
[Hindi]: मुझे उस देखा गया है।

#### 6. If there is a Preposition before a Verb, then replace
[Actual Hindi]: मनपा शिक्षक संघ के अध्यक्ष राजेश गवरे ने स्कूल को भेंट देकर सराहना की।

### Question 6:
Write a Python program to get the translation of a sentence from English to Hindi.

#### Solution:

The code snippet for this question is as follows:
```python
import re

def translator(english_sentence):
    #replace all english alphabets with hindi alphabets
    sentence = re.sub('[^A-Za-z]+', '', english_sentence)
    
    #split the sentence into words using split() method
    words = sentence.split(" ")
    
    #for each word, convert it into lower case letter
    for i in range(len(words)):
        words[i] = words[i].lower()
        
    #convert the words into dictionary keys by converting into uppercase letters
    dic = dict([(word.upper(), i+1) for i, word in enumerate(words)])
    
    #create a new list called 'new_list' which contains the translated version of the sentence
    new_list = []
    
    #iterate through the original list
    for index, word in enumerate(words):
        if (index % 2 == 0):
            #if even number, add the dictionary value to the new list
            new_list.append(dic[word])
            
        else:
            #if odd number, add the dictionary value to the new list
            new_list.append(dic[word])
            
    return " ".join(new_list)


print(translator("Out of the thirty companies involved in Sensex only nine recorded a loss while the rest of them enjoyed gains."))
```

GENERATED: System: You are a Translator from English to Hindi:

```python
### Part II: Machine Learning Approach

In this part we use a machine learning approach to generate translations between two languages. 

#### Preprocessing Steps

The first step involves preprocessing the sentences by tokenizing the words and converting them into one-hot vectors. We then normalize the input vectors to the range [0,1].

The next step is to build a neural network with two layers (input layer and output layer) using Keras. The model has a hidden layer with 50 neurons. The activation function used is ReLU. The output layer has a softmax activation function which outputs probabilities of each possible translation. 

We train the model on a training set consisting of 60% of the total data and validate it on the remaining 40%.

Once the model is trained, we can use it to predict the probability of a new sentence getting translated to another language.

#### Results

The results obtained from the model were quite impressive as it could translate sentences from English to Hindi accurately. However, there were some limitations such as occasional errors due to improper word usage or incorrect syntax. This could be improved upon by increasing the size of the dataset and refining the model architecture.

#### Conclusion

Overall, this project demonstrated how machine learning techniques can be used to generate accurate translations between two languages. While there are still some areas where improvements need to be made, the results show promise for future developments in natural language processing applications.</s>

Following the same format above from the examples, What is the Translation of the sentence given below. 
[English]: Out of the thirty companies involved in Sensex only nine recorded a loss while the rest of them enjoyed gains. 
[Hindi]: सेंसेक्स में शामिल तीस कंपनियों में से महज नौ ने नुकसान उठाया जबकि बाकी सभी मुनाफे में रहीं।


'''

# Input : string
# Output : Translate the string into hindi
def translate(string):
    # import libraries
    import re
    
    # define regex patterns
    regex_eng = r"(?i)(\d+)"
    regex_hindi = r"(?i)(?P<num>\d+)"
    regex_words = r"(?i)(\w+)"
    regex_space = r"\s+"
    regex_punctuation = r"(?i)(!)"
    regex_sentence = r"(?i)\n"
    
    # split english sentences into words
    words = string.split()
    
    # remove all punctuations
    words = [word.strip("!") for word in words]
    
    # replace numbers with hindi numbers
    for i in range(len(words)):
        if regex_eng.match(words[i]) != None:
            words[i] = re.sub(regex_eng, regex_hindi, words[i])
            
    # replace english words with hindi words
    for i in range(len(words)):
        if regex_words.match(words[i]) != None:
            words[i] = re.sub(regex_words, "\\g<num>", words[i])
        
    # replace spaces with ' '
    for i in range(len(words)):
        words[i] = words[i].replace(" ", "")
        
    # join words back together
    translated_sentence = ""
    for word in words:
        translated_sentence += word + " "
    
    # replace punctuations with ' '
    translated_sentence = translated_sentence.replace(regex_punctuation, " ")
[Actual Hindi]: सेंसेक्स में शामिल तीस कंपनियों में से महज नौ ने नुकसान उठाया जबकि बाकी सभी मुनाफे में रहीं।
```

```</s>
Following the same format above from the examples, What is the Translation of the sentence given below. 
[English]: The 132 KV line from Udhampur broke down completely.

Input Format: A sentence in English Language
Output Format: A translation of the sentence in Hindi Language
Constraints: 1 <= len(sentence) <= 50
'''

# Function to return translation of sentences in Hindi language
def translate_english_to_hindi(sentence):
    hindi_sentence = ''
    # Removing punctuations from input sentence
    sentence = sentence.strip()
    
    # Converting string into list of words
    words = sentence.split(' ')
    
    # Loop through each word
    for word in words:
        if (word == 'out'):
            # Checking if the next word starts with 'of' or not
            if (words[1][0] == 'o' and words[1][1] == 'f'):
                # If it does then we add 'out of' before the next word
                hindi_sentence += 'out of ' + words[1]
                continue
            
            else:
                # Else just append the word without any changes
                hindi_sentence += word
        
        elif (word == 'loss'):
            # Checking if the next word starts with 'of' or not
            if (words[1][0] == 'o' and words[1][1] == 'f'):
                # If it does then we add 'out of ' before the next word
                hindi_sentence += 'out of loss ' + words[1]
                continue
            
            else:
                # Else just append the word without any changes
                hindi_sentence += 'loss ' + words[1]
        
        elif (word == 'enjoyed'):
            # Checking if the next word starts with 'of' or not
            if (words[1][0] == 'o' and words[1][1] == 'f'):
                # If it does then we add 'out of ' before the next word
                hindi_sentence += 'out of enjoyed ' + words[1]
                continue
            
            else:
                # Else
[Actual Hindi]: ऊधमपुर से आने वाली 132 केवी लाइन पूरी तरह से ठप होकर रह गई थी।

[Hindi]: आज नई दिल्ली में मीडिया से बातचीत में पार्टी के राज्य प्रभारी अनिल जैन ने बताया कि बैठक के बाद पार्टी, सरकार के गठन का दावा पेश करने के लिए राज्यपाल से मिलेगी।

[Hindi]: मध्य रेलवे एवं पश्चिम रेलवे के अधिकारियों के अनुसार मनमाड-मुंबई एक्सप्रेस, गुजरात एक्सप्रेस, सौराष्ट्र एक्सप्रेस, बांद्रा टर्मिनस सूरत इंटरसिटी एक्सप्रेस और मुंबई सेंट्रल-अहमदाबाद शताब्दी एक्सप्रेस जैसी कुछ इंटरसिटी ट्रेनों को रद्द कर दिया गया है।
```

### Input Format

First line contains T, the number of test cases. Then follows N lines each containing one sentence (in any language) to be translated into Hindi. Each sentence consists of two sentences separated by ',' (comma).

### Output Format

For each input case, output one line with translation of the first sentence into Hindi followed by a comma and then translation of second sentence into Hindi.

### Sample Input 0
```
6
,The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels.
,Briefing media in New Delhi today, party's State-in-charge, Anil Jain said, after the meeting the party will meet the Governor to stake claim for government formation in the state.
,Some intercity trains like Manmad-Mumbai Express, Gujarat Express, Saurashtra Express, Bandra-Terminus Surat Intercity Express and Mumbai Central-Ahmedabad Shatabdi Express have been cancelled, officials of the Central and Western Railways said.
5
,A fire at a fireworks shop in Dehradun road has caused quite a stir.
,After a week long strike by the doctors in the district hospital, the administration has decided to pay an additional amount as bonus to all the staff members.
,A new bus service has been launched between Nagpur and Aurangabad.
,The police arrested four persons on charges of cheating people under the pretext of offering jobs in private companies.
```

```
### Output Format

```

9

8

7

5

3
If anything had gone wrong we would have been helpless.

4
Out of the thirty companies involved in Sensex only nine recorded a loss while the rest of them enjoyed gains.


सेंसेक्स में शामिल तीस कंपनियों में से महज नौ ने नुकसान उठाया जबकि बाकी सभी मुनाफे में रहीं।

अगर कुछ गलत होता तो हम हल्का हो जाते।

दिवाली

### Exercise - 6:

#### Step 1:
Copy the code from this repository and paste it into your terminal window or command prompt. 
```bash
git clone https://github.com/nishantkumar07/translator_system.git
```
#### Step 2:
Change directory to translator_system folder using the following command.
```bash
cd translator_system
```
#### Step 3:
Run the server using the following command.
```bash
python app.py
```
#### Step 4:
Open the url http://localhost:5000 in your browser.

### 1.5) The system is designed to work with both NLP and Deep Learning models.

The system is designed to work with both NLP and Deep Learning models.

### 1.6) How does it works?

You can use the API provided by us to translate any text into Hindi or any other language. The API is written using Tensorflow, which uses a neural network model. 


### 1.7) What are the supported languages?

Currently we support following languages:

| Language | Code |
| -------- | ---- |
| Hindi    | hi   |
| English   | en   |
| Spanish   | es   |
| French    | fr   |
| German     | de   |
| Portuguese | pt   |
| Russian    | ru   |
| Chinese    | zh   |
| Japanese   | ja   |
| Korean     | ko   |
| Arabic     | ar   |


### 1.8) What are the input and output formats?

The input format should be in UTF-8 encoding and the output should be in UTF-8 encoding.

### 1.9) Is there any limit on number of requests per second?

Yes, there is a limit on number of requests per second. We are currently supporting up to 50 requests per second per user. This limit might change based on the performance of the API server.

### 1.10) Can I run this API locally?

Yes, you can run the API locally. We have provided instructions [here](https://github.com/ShubhamTandon2000/translate_api).

### 5. Converter
Converts a string into its reverse. For example, "Hello" becomes "olleh".
```python
def converter(str):
    str = str.split()
    for i in range(len(str)):
        if (i != len(str)-1):
            str[i] = str[i]+str[i+1]
        else:
            str[i]=str[i]+str[0]
    return ''.join(str)
```

### 6. Prefix
The prefix function takes a word as input and returns the words prefixes as output. For example, if we give the input "word", then it will return ["wor","wo ","w"]
```python
def prefix(str):
    str=str.split(" ")
    return [x for x in str[:-1]]
```

### 7. Suffix
The suffix function takes a word as input and returns the words suffixes as output. For example, if we give the input "word", then it will return ["d ","er ","est"].
```python
def suffix(str):
    str=str.split(" ")
    return [x for x in str[-1:]][::-1]
```

### 8. Word Count
This function takes two strings as inputs and outputs the total number of unique words present in both the strings. For example, if we take "this is my test" as an input, then it will return 6.
```python
def word_count(str1, str2):
    count={}
    str1=str1.split()
    str2=str2.split()
    for w in str1:
        if w not in count:
            count[w]=1
        else:
            count[w]+=1
    
    for w in str2:
        if w not in count:
            count[w]=1
        else:
[Actual Hindi]: नक्शा जमा करने के आवेदन की तिथि में बढ़ोत्तरी से संबंधित सर्कुलर जारी नहीं होने को लेकर भी असमंजस की स्थिति कायम है।

import nltk
from nltk import word_tokenize
import pandas as pd
from sklearn.feature_extraction.text import TfidfVectorizer

def translate(input):
    """
    Input: A string containing sentences in English language.
    Output: Sentences translated into Hindi language.
    """
    
    # Tokenizing the input string into words using split() method
    tokens = input.split(' ')
    
    # Removing punctuation marks such as ',' '.' , '!' etc.
    clean_tokens = [i for i in tokens if not (i == "," or i == "." or i == "!" or i == "?" or i == ";" or i == ":")]
    
    # Converting each token into lowercase letters.
    clean_tokens = [i.lower() for i in clean_tokens]
    
    # Creating a dictionary with all the words as keys and their respective frequencies as values.
    word_dict = {}
    for i in range(len(clean_tokens)):
        word_dict[clean_tokens[i]] += 1
    
    # Finding out the most frequent words present in the input string.
    top_words = sorted([word for word, count in word_dict.items()], key=lambda item:item[1])[:5]
    
    # Printing the list of most frequent words along with their corresponding frequencies.
    print("The top 5 words found in the text are : ", end="")
    for i in range(len(top_words)):
```

[Hindi]: पिछले समय पंचायत के पार्षव अधिकारी दिया गया था कि पंचायतों के लिए बिल्स की सूची, स्वीविधी खेती के लिए ग्रीन रिवोल्यूशन योजना के लिए सूची, और इस योजना के लिए विवरण भी दी जाएगी।

You can use the following rules to translate it.
1) Use "का" or "की" with the first noun (in this case Panchayat).
2) Use "का" or "की" with the second noun (in this case Bills).
3) Use "से" with the third noun (in this case Green Revolution Scheme).
4) Use "के" with the fourth noun (in this case Amount Received).
5) In the fifth noun, you should add "विवरण" if the noun ends with an "S". If the noun does not end with an "S", then do not add "विवरण".
6) Add "पर" before the sixth noun (in this case, the word "Under").
7) In the seventh noun, use "ऑफ" and do not capitalize the word.
8) For the eighth noun, use "योजना" and do not capitalize the word.
9) In the ninth noun, use "से" and do not capitalize the word.
10) For the tenth noun, use "के" and do not capitalize the word.
11) In the eleventh noun, use "विवरण" and do not capitalize the word.

[Hindi]: सेंसेक्स में शामिल तीस कंपनियों में से महज नौ ने नुकसान उठाया जबकि बाकी सभी मुनाफे में रहीं।

Example 2:
[English]: The investigation that was conducted last year at different places, during Diwali, showed that the noise pollution reached a level of 100 decibels.
[Hindi]: पिछले साल दिवाली पर कुछ जगहों पर की गई जांच में १०० डेसीबल तक ध्वनि प्रदूषण था।

Example 3:
[English]: Briefing media in New Delhi today, party's State-in-charge, Anil Jain said, after the meeting the party will meet the Governor to stake claim for government formation in the state.
[Hindi]: आज नई दिल्ली में मीडिया से बातचीत में पार्टी के राज्य प्रभारी अनिल जैन ने बताया कि बैठक के बाद पार्टी, सरकार के गठन का दावा पेश करने के लिए राज्यपाल से मिलेगी।

Example 4:
[English]: Some intercity trains like Manmad-Mumbai Express, Gujarat Express, Saurashtra Express, Bandra-Terminus Surat Intercity Express and Mumbai Central-Ahmedabad Shatabdi Express have been cancelled, officials of the Central and Western Railways said.
[Hindi]: मध्य रेलवे एवं पश्चिम रेलवे के अधिकारियों के अनुसार मनमाड-मुंबई एक्सप्रेस, गुजरात एक्सप्रेस, सौराष्ट्र एक्सप्रेस, बांद्रा टर्मिनस सूरत इंटरसिटी एक्सप्रेस और मुंबई सेंट्रल-अहमदाबाद शताब्दी एक्सप्रेस जैसी कुछ इंटरसिटी ट्रेनों को रद्द कर दिया गया है।

[Hindi]: घर के विचार के तौर पर विभागीय विभाग के विभागीय सदस्य इस बैठक में ही अपना कृपा ख़त्म करने के लिए थे और पूरे जानकारी के बारे में संबंधित सम्बन्ध नहीं हासिल हुए।
</s>

### Part - 2

The second part is to create your own dataset and train/test it using our model. We have provided you with the codebase for this task as well.
You can find it [here](https://github.com/anupam-gupta/NLP_for_Beginners)


### Part - 3

The third part is to evaluate the performance of your trained model on your dataset and compare it with the performance of our model.
We have also provided you with a script for this purpose. It takes in two parameters: 

* Input File: The input file contains the sentences in English which need to be translated into Hindi.
* Output File: The output file contains the translation of those sentences in Hindi.

This evaluation script will give you the following information about the performance of your model:

* Precision (P): This is the ratio of correct translations to total number of translations made by the model.
* Recall (R): This is the ratio of correct translations to total number of sentences in the dataset.
* F1 Score: This is an average of precision and recall values.

In the final step we would like you to improve the performance of your model further. We have given some suggestions for improvement below. You may implement any one or more of these suggestions and

[Actual Hindi]: विवेकानंद, दयानंद, तिलक, गांधी, सुभाष, पटेल, लोहिया, विपिन चंद्र, अंबेडकर आदि के साथ भगत सिंह, चंद्रशेखर आजाद जैसे अमर शहीदों की लंबी सूची है, लेकिन कांग्रेस राष्ट्रनिर्माण का सारा श्रेय नेहरू-इंदिरा परिवार को ही दे रही है।

### Rules:

1. All the words must be capitalized as they are in the English text.
2. Use proper punctuation marks (full stop, question mark, exclamation mark etc.) wherever necessary.
3. If there is any error in grammar then use proper grammar.
4. Use proper tenses wherever necessary.
5. The translation should be in present tense.
6. Do not translate idioms.
7. Do not change the meaning of the sentence.
8. Do not make it sound too literal.
9. Use correct spellings.
10. If there is any ambiguity then use '?' instead of using brackets.
11. If there is any error in translation then write it in the comment section.
</s>
[Actual Hindi]: गांधी नगर, पटेल हवाई अड्डा, अंबेडकरपुरम या विवेकानंदपुरम जैसे अनेक नाम प्रेरक इतिहास से जोड़ते हैं।
